width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.424em; left: 0.986em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-861" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">4</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-862" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">N</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 5.412em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -4.348em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 5.502em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">l</mi></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi><mrow><mn>0.1</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></mrow></mfrac><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mo>×</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>−</mo><mn>6</mn></mrow></msup><mo>×</mo><mn>0.1</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mfrac><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>11</mn></mrow></msup><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>−</mo><mn>6</mn></mrow></msup><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>10</mn></mrow><mn>4</mn></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">N</mi></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-95">\rm Y=\frac{F}{A}\times \frac{L}{l}\Rightarrow Y=\frac{F}{A}\times\frac{L}{0.1L}  \\

\Rightarrow Y=\frac{F\times1}{1\times{10}^{-6}\times0.1\times1}\  
\\ \Rightarrow F=2\times{10}^{11}\times{10}^{-6}\times{10}^{-1}=2\times{10}^4N 
</script></span><br>
